<div id="review_478138643" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/478138643" />
    <a title="Paula " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2879703-paula"><img alt="Paula " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536687412p2/2879703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/478138643?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paula " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paula " href="/user/show/2879703-paula">Paula </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478138643" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10057369513858752290"><br/><i>The Proposal</i> is the highly anticipated sequel to <i>The Proposition</i> and is NOT a stand-alone. You must read <i>The Proposition</i> first before you even read this review or you will read spoilers from the first book. <br/><br/><i>
  <b>“A hopeful look entered his tortured eyes. “I’d give anything and everything in this world to redeem myself with you. Just please, please give me the chance.”</b>
</i><br/><br/>After the shocking ending of the first book, I was anxiously awaiting to see what happens with Aidan and Emma. I was extremely mad </span>
  <span id="freeText10057369513858752290" style="display:none"><br /><i>The Proposal</i> is the highly anticipated sequel to <i>The Proposition</i> and is NOT a stand-alone. You must read <i>The Proposition</i> first before you even read this review or you will read spoilers from the first book. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>“A hopeful look entered his tortured eyes. “I’d give anything and everything in this world to redeem myself with you. Just please, please give me the chance.”</b>
</i><br /><br />After the shocking ending of the first book, I was anxiously awaiting to see what happens with Aidan and Emma. I was extremely mad at Aidan for his foolish mistake. I wanted Aidan on his knees groveling for Emma's forgiveness. The man not only paid the price for what he did, but he exceeded my begging expectations. And I fell even more in love with Aidan in <i>The Proposal.</i><br /><br />In the beginning of the story, Aidan is still in the dog house. He's miserable and struggling with losing Emma. He's lost sleep, lost weight, and drinking excessively. He's tried everything from begging in text messages to sending a whole florists shop of flowers to win Emma back. But, he didn't just break Emma's heart, he crushed it into a million pieces.<br /><br />Emma is not sure if she <i>even</i> wants Aidan back. She may love him, but she can't forget how he shattered her heart and her trust. So, she avoids Aidan at all cost and has cut off all communication with him. Yet, no matter how angry she is with Aidan, she still desperately misses him.<br /><br />When Emma is suddenly put on strict bed rest six months into her pregnancy, Aidan eagerly steps in to take care of her. He does everything in his power, including taking a leave of absence from work, to make sure she is comfortable and well cared for. He even willingly goes out at one in the morning to get her a Wendy's fix.(Now, that's how you woo a pregnant woman!) With these little gestures of affection, Aidan continuously proves himself more and more how much he is willing to sacrifice for Emma and his unborn son, Noah. He wanted nothing more than to have his family back. And it didn't take long before I had forgiven Aidan. But, even though he won me over, Emma and Aidan had a lot of problems to work through before they could be together. <br /><br />I really didn't care for the part of the story with the doctor. Pesh is an ER doctor Emma met while in the hospital. When they first meet, there is an immediate attraction between the two. And when Emma accepts Pesh’s offer to check up on her at Aidan's house and also bring her dinner, I have to admit, by this point, I was exasperated with Emma. I kept thinking, "What are you doing woman?!" *sigh* I guess this time around, it was Emma's turn to be the idiot. All I wanted was Aidan, Aidan, and only Aidan to be in the picture. I do realize that Aidan really hurt her but, her actions were starting to mirror what Aidan did to her. It's ironic how I went from being furious with Aidan in the first book, to wanting nothing more than for Emma to admit that Aidan is the one and only man she wanted. <br /><br />But, alas, things did turn around by the second half of the book. I really enjoyed how sweet and romantic this part of the story was. It was much more enjoyable than the first half where I felt completely on edge and annoyed. Aidan, true to his word, came through for Emma. He proved his love. He proved she could trust him. He proved that he wasn't a complete scumbag after all. And he <i>finally</i> says those three little words that mean so much to Emma. So, Aidan does get to keep his thingie that I threatened in my first review. This once womanizing scoundrel really grew up in this story and became the best kind of man. And it didn't take the whole book for this couple to work their problems out. Hallelujah!<br /><br /><i>The Proposal</i> is the perfect ending to Emma and Aidan's story. Tears, laughter, pain, and anger were all a part of their journey to finding what they were both looking for. Happiness. <br /><br />Rating: B<br />Heat: Hot<br /><br />-- <i>A <a href="http://romanticbookaffairs.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Romantic Book Affairs</a> Review</i><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Find us on <a href="https://twitter.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> and <a href="http://facebook.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> too!</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Thank you Katie Ashley for kindly providing the ARC. Romantic Book Affairs loves you! :) </span>
  <a data-text-id="10057369513858752290" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2429463960487777873">Pre-reading: Aidan you better make things right in this one or someone won't see the next dawn...<br/><br/>After reading the book: Aidan you are lucky and I won't kill you. Somehow I couldn't be mad at Aidan for cheating, which is not something I do usually, and I was hoping he was going to get her back with some grand gesture. But the grand gestures are n</span>
  <span id="freeText2429463960487777873" style="display:none">Pre-reading: Aidan you better make things right in this one or someone won't see the next dawn...<br /><br />After reading the book: Aidan you are lucky and I won't kill you. Seriously I wasn't expecting all the things he did to get Emma back. He showed her how sweet and caring he is and that he is going to be there for her. Somehow I couldn't be mad at Aidan for cheating, which is not something I do usually, and I was hoping he was going to get her back with some grand gesture. But the grand gestures are not what Emma needs or gets. The small things Aidan does are the one that matter in the end. <br /><br />And then Pesh comes into the scenery and is after Emma's heart. I am team Aidan and if I want to be honest the doctor is pretty good but I didn't like him with Emma and let's just say that if he died somehow(see Grey's Anatomy)I wouldn't be unhappy or would give him a second thought. That was until he said the quote below and then mostly disappeared from Emma and Aidan's life. The quote made me like him a little and later it helped when he did a favor to Emma.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I want you to think about this for a minute? What would you rather have? Words that can be spoken lightly and then taken back so easily, or would you rather actions?”</i>
</b><br /><br />There isn't a triangle in the book, just a hormonal woman who wants to protect her heart from breaking again and a safe choice coming into her life. Because Pesh is the safe choice the one that wouldn't threaten her heart and Aidan is the unsafe one. What guarantees her that he won't hurt her again? So I can't or you really blame her for trying something with Pesh.<br />What I can blame her sort of is not appreciating what Aidan did to win her over and brushing it off nothing while she was at his place and he was taking care of her. <br /><br />The proposal, anticipated by many, is the end of Emma and Aidan's story. It had me worried for a second that the end would be different in some way and I was glad to see that that wasn't the case.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13392828124338584670">You guys!<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/418067.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ah! That was such a great ending to this amazing story! Yay! Can you tell I'm happy? Can you? CAN YOU? lol<br/><br/>Let's see... what can I tell you guys about it...<br/><br/>So if you remember right I was left more than just freaking out at the end of <i>The Proposition</i> [<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/434655081' rel='nofollow noopener'>review</a>] so excuse me for dying to read the sequel. Gah. The waiting was terrible. Actually, I think it's the worst cliffie I've had to live through. Ever!<br/><br/>Okay. Moving on.<br/><br/>In <i>The Proposal</i> we have Emma and Aidan back, but with a major brick wal</span>
  <span id="freeText13392828124338584670" style="display:none">You guys!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/418067.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ah! That was such a great ending to this amazing story! Yay! Can you tell I'm happy? Can you? CAN YOU? lol<br><br>Let's see... what can I tell you guys about it...<br><br>So if you remember right I was left more than just freaking out at the end of <i>The Proposition</i> [<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/434655081" rel="nofollow noopener">review</a>] so excuse me for dying to read the sequel. Gah. The waiting was terrible. Actually, I think it's the worst cliffie I've had to live through. Ever!<br><br>Okay. Moving on.<br><br>In <i>The Proposal</i> we have Emma and Aidan back, but with a major brick wall between them, aka Aidan's ass cheating move. Yup. So maybe I was a little angry at what he did before, but I'm all on forgiving, especially if he's... you know, as perfect as Aidan is! *cough*<br><br>So now he has to do everything is his power to get Emma back, for both their sakes as well as their soon-to-be-born son. But that might be a little bit harder than expected, heh Aidan? Mhmm. Emma is a hard woman to convince. And <em>duh!</em> He totally deserved to do some serious groveling.<br><br>Yet that's not everything Aidan is against. There's also the issue of the new doctor, Pesh, having the hots for Emma... Okay, so maybe he didn't have the hots for Emma... <i>maybe,</i> but he wanted to steal her from my Aidan and that's a no-no!<br><br>Even worse! Emma was willing to give him a chance! Okay, so she's hurt, I get it, but I did not appreciate her moves, I mean...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400272ra/775438.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I mentioned this on my pre-review (which is now gone) that I kind of, sort of... maybe disliked Pesh without even having read about him, a tiny little bit. And well, he didn't turn out to be so bad, once he was out-of-the-way for Emma and Aidan that is, because meanwhile he was both mine and Aidan's mortal enemy.<br><br>Okay I'm only kidding. <s>Maybe.</s><br><br>Anyways. Even though I didn't find <i>The Proposal</i> to be quite as good as the previous book, it was still really good and worth the wait. If for nothing else, to at least not be left in the agony of not knowing how everything was going to turn out. ;)<br><br>Aidan was again swoon-worthy, even more with his added sweetness and protection when Emma really needed him. Being a daddy sure suited him well. ;) Emma kind of got on my bad side sometimes, I don't even know why. It was obvious she couldn't forgive him on the blink of an eye (I would totally slap her if she did) but I found myself pouting when she just wouldn't give Aidan a chance, and then there was the Pesh-moments to bother me further. We are good now, though. I forgave her. *wink*<br><br>And that's it. I'm kind of sad it's over. *pout* But go ahead, and get some Aidan for yourself!<br><br><img alt="" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394382ra/759345.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer453788538" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16751807461891176881">The story of Aidan and Emma continues...<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&current=ProposalAIdan.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783837i/450623.jpg' alt='Aidan' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&current=ProposalEmma.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397313i/766500.jpg' alt='Emma' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i>“I want you to think about this for a minute. What would you rather have? Words that can be spoken lightly and then taken back so easily, or would you rather have actions?” </i>
</b><br/><br/>The Proposal starts off right where The Proposition left off... the first half of the book had me all over the place, it was angsty- had me upset, happy, sad, nervous, then the second half- ahhhh sweet relief! Sexy and romantic! Overall, loved the whole book!!!<br/><br/>Aidan screwed </span>
  <span id="freeText16751807461891176881" style="display:none">The story of Aidan and Emma continues...<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=ProposalAIdan.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379783837i/450623.jpg" alt="Aidan" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/albums/y537/Christyb23/?action=view&amp;current=ProposalEmma.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397313i/766500.jpg" alt="Emma" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“I want you to think about this for a minute. What would you rather have? Words that can be spoken lightly and then taken back so easily, or would you rather have actions?” </i>
</b><br><br>The Proposal starts off right where The Proposition left off... the first half of the book had me all over the place, it was angsty- had me upset, happy, sad, nervous, then the second half- ahhhh sweet relief! Sexy and romantic! Overall, loved the whole book!!!<br><br>Aidan screwed up. Big time. And he knows it. He has begged and pleaded with Emma to forgive him, but nothing seems to be working. She gets put on bedrest for two weeks and Aidan volunteers to have her at his house to take care of her, and boy does he! <br><b>
  <i>“I’d give anything and everything in this world to redeem myself with you. Just please, give me the chance.”</i>
</b><br>He really starts to wear Emma down with his kindness, but then steps in Dr. Pesh, the ER doctor who treated Emma... I didn’t want to like Pesh, but I kinda did. As long as he kept his hands off Emma. Loved Aidan’s description of him though! <br><b>
  <i>It wasn’t the fact that Dr. Nadeen had the looks that made women’s panties ignite, but the fucker was kind and considerate. Throw in the fact that he was a doctor, and he was a triple threat. </i>
</b><br>Pesh was a nice guy, and I hope he finds love, but I have to say- I was Team Aidan 100%! After a lot of angst, I got some happy :D Finally, what I’ve been waiting for- both books to happen, did! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>
    <b>“Please, Em. I love you so much it hurts. I ache for you in my soul. Please... I can’t live without you. I want to be with you every minute of every day. I want to marry you and make a life with you. I want to raise Noah together and be a family together. Please... please say you want to be with me forever.”</b>
  </i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>Oh swooooon Aidan! You are wonderful!!!<br><br>Love Aidan and Emma, and of course Patrick! He is one of my favorite characters, such a sweetheart! Emma’s best friend Casey and Aidan’s nephews were also great and hilarious!!!<br><i>“Oh for fucks sake! Wake him up and let him show off his shiny new vag!”<br>“Casey know I wear my alleged vagina with pride, not because she took my manhood with that purse of hers, but because I want to be a better man for you.”<br>Cad= “A dude that acts like a douchebag to women.”- One of Aidan’s nephews </i> <br><br>A great contemporary romance. The ending was perfect! Loved it! Read this one!!!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_460948966" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/460948966" />
    <a title="Anne OK" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/285610-anne-ok"><img alt="Anne OK" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505981069p2/285610.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/460948966?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anne OK" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anne OK" href="/user/show/285610-anne-ok">Anne OK</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/285610-anne-ok?shelf=2013-reads">2013-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer460948966" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer165193082547682558">He’s a screw up – yep Aidan did a bad, bad thing. Now he’s got to grovel and beg and plead to make things right with Emma. And Emma isn’t going to make it easy for him! She’s even going to consider casting him aside forever in favor of another man. Whoa! Don’t think for one minute that Aidan is going to let that happen – at least not without giving everything he’s got in him to turn the tables around. The character of Pesh was probably my least favorite aspect about this story. I just didn’t fin</span>
  <span id="freeText165193082547682558" style="display:none">He’s a screw up – yep Aidan did a bad, bad thing. Now he’s got to grovel and beg and plead to make things right with Emma. And Emma isn’t going to make it easy for him! She’s even going to consider casting him aside forever in favor of another man. Whoa! Don’t think for one minute that Aidan is going to let that happen – at least not without giving everything he’s got in him to turn the tables around. The character of Pesh was probably my least favorite aspect about this story. I just didn’t find him believable. For me, he was just a little too “perfect.” I loved watching Aidan’s determination at work even while confronted with so many really squirm-worthy hurdles.<br /><br />Katie Ashley does a flipping good job at writing sassy dialogue, tempting and delicious characters, along with an award-winning cast of delightful secondary characters that sometimes keep you laughing out loud. There’s a mixture of young and old who add such a real and special feeling to this series. I would be remiss in not giving special attention to one of my very favorite secondary characters in both “The Proposition” and “The Proposal,” a loyal and loving dog named Beau. Love you, boy!<br /><br />And oh yes, the romance is off-the-charts wickedly good. The chemistry between Aidan and Emma is hot, sensuous, and compelling. There are also some very funny and comical moments thrown in as well. The special moments contribute to making their relationship so much more real and enjoyable. Noah Patrick’s arrival was the icing on the cake. Ashley brought out the best in all concerned. She gave tender meaning to the moment of truth in this story. And the addition of a superb and wonderful Epilogue supported a fully satisfying Happily-Ever-After. <br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /> <br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="165193082547682558" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_478055302" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/478055302" />
    <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr"><img alt="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1465384674p2/9080319.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/478055302?book_show_action=true">Dec 15, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️" href="/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr">Allison ❤️Will Never Conquer Her TBR❤️</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer478055302" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11210884058723473345">The continued story of Emma and Aiden. The first book in the series ends with Aiden hurting Em by hooking up with a girl (being caught before the deed). His fear of commitment and doing this to sabotage his relationship with Emma, he suddenly realizes she's all he wants.....her and baby Noah. And he's willing to go all out to prove to her that she can trust him.<br/><br/>Suddenly Aiden's dad has heart problems. The stress of it in the hospital puts Emma into preterm labor. Her doctors orders- strict bedre</span>
  <span id="freeText11210884058723473345" style="display:none">The continued story of Emma and Aiden. The first book in the series ends with Aiden hurting Em by hooking up with a girl (being caught before the deed). His fear of commitment and doing this to sabotage his relationship with Emma, he suddenly realizes she's all he wants.....her and baby Noah. And he's willing to go all out to prove to her that she can trust him.<br /><br />Suddenly Aiden's dad has heart problems. The stress of it in the hospital puts Emma into preterm labor. Her doctors orders- strict bedrest and no stress- or orgasms. Aiden eagerly takes on the challenge of caring for her, taking 2 weeks of work. While in the hospital she also meets an ER doc Dr Nadeem. Woah. She's got instant chemistry with him and he asks for her number and if he can do house calls. How's this going to work while she's staying at Aidens? <br /><br />This was a good read. Not a ton of action or new details to their story, really. Just the day to day struggle between Aiden and Emma and rebuilding the trust that was lost from his indiscretions from book one. The bedrest makes for no sex so much of the book was chaste with very little hot moments during that time. I think the author could've put more angsty "I want you but we can't do it" moments just to spice it up a bit. <br /><br />I love Aiden. He was a douchenozzle in book one ending but I loved his tenacity to make things right by Emma. It's a good fluffy read. Not quite as good as the first in the series but I still enjoyed it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11210884058723473345" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_16041169'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16041169-disastrous"><img alt="Disastrous (Disastrous, #1)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1348436233l/16041169._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TMYCbGCyiEJHrrE1/NENkEp/NRTDiNxllHsfxZPyb55f0zO3ZXQelzvgSViDejq+0SCPYiND+kApsu9RLs54oA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Vljkjr24H4gRrKAqPt8iAgi7bk0wem5lTOt+/IJbL79FTdVVuH6JXW3iWEdBdBUsk+TUO9CxSEDxIo5oP2c4gQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText2890142479137506611" style="display:none">Katie Ashley is a New York Times, USA Today, and Amazon Top Three Best-Selling author of both Indie and Traditionally published books. She's written rockers, bikers, manwhores with hearts of gold, New Adult, and Young Adult. She lives outside of Atlanta, Georgia with her daughter, Olivia, her rescue mutts, Belle and Elsa, and her two cats, Mama Kitty and Luna. She has a slight obsession with The Golden Girls, Shakespeare, Harry Potter, and Star Wars. <br /><br />With a BA in English, a BS in Secondary English Education, and a Masters in Adolescent English Education, she spent eleven years teaching both middle and high school English, as well as a few adjunct college English classes. As of January 2013, she became a full-time writer.<br /><br />Although she is a life-long Georgia peach, she loves traveling the country and world meeting readers.
